<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h1><strong>A statement from our founder</strong><br/> Jeffrey M. Smith</h1>
<p style="text-align: left;"><strong>We</strong> believe that GMOs—and the Roundup herbicide sprayed on them—promote disease.</p>
<p>We’ve caught Bayer/Monsanto and others rigging their research and covering up dangers. Now, with cheap new techniques that are prone to side-effects, the industry is engineering anything with DNA: from algae to animals, from fungus to fish. This “Gene Rush” could replace nature in this generation. It’s our duty to investigate, expose, and act.</p>
<p class="attribution" style="text-align: right;">– Jeffrey Smith</p></div>
</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_button_module_wrapper et_pb_button_8_wrapper et_pb_module">

</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_19 about-jeffrey-box et_clickable et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3 style="text-align: left; font-style: normal; font-size: 16px; line-height: 155%;">The leading consumer advocate promoting healthier non-GMO choices, <a class="teal-link" href="https://www.responsibletechnology.org/about/jeffrey-m-smith-biography/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Jeffrey Smith</a> was named the 2017 “Person of the Year” by Masters of Health Magazine. For more than two decades, his research has exposed how biotech companies mislead policy makers and the public, and put the health of society and environment at risk.</h3></div>
</div> <!-- .et_pb_text --><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_20 et_clickable et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3 style="text-align: left; font-style: normal; font-size: 18px; line-height: 155%;">The leading consumer advocate promoting healthier non-GMO choices, <a class="teal-link" href="https://www.responsibletechnology.org/about/jeffrey-m-smith-biography/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Jeffrey Smith</a> was named the 2017 “Person of the Year” by Masters of Health Magazine. For more than two decades, his research has exposed how biotech companies mislead policy makers and the public, and put the health of society and environment at risk.</h3></div>
